# Ecommerce Ops — Improvement Journal

> **Purpose.** Chronological log of every bounded improvement the cron job makes to `/data/workspace/ecommerce-ops/`. Each entry is one tick — what shipped, why, what to do next. The next agent reads this on wakeup to pick up where the last tick left off.
>
> **Format.** Newest at top. Each tick gets a `## [YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM] <one-line title>` block with: what changed, files touched, TDD evidence, next-action.

## [2026-06-27 14:30] Playbook seed — Marketplace Launch (4-phase Amazon + Walmart + Target Plus + EU marketplaces operator build; canonical 2nd-layer follow-up to research/06-marketplace-expansion.md per the research → playbook → asset → operator-surface → scripts → static-dashboard layer order; Move #13 from research/03 line 178; 8.3:1 default Year-1 ROI Path B at $5M US GMV base)

- **What shipped:** `playbooks/13-marketplace-launch.md` (new, **74KB / 562 lines / the 18th playbook in the workspace** + the canonical 2nd-layer operator-build companion for the marketplace-expansion track per the canonical research → playbook → asset → operator-surface → scripts → static-dashboard layer order; Move #13 from `research/03-30-day-rollout-plan.md` line 178 + the canonical next-pick per `research/06-marketplace-expansion.md` line 7 + line 397 + the prior tick's `docs/journal.md` next-action recommendation). The playbook ships the canonical 4-phase marketplace-launch operator build across Amazon + Walmart + Target Plus + EU marketplaces: **(a) Phase 1 — Amazon-only (US 3P + FBA) ~25 hr Weeks 1–4** with a 9-step build [USPTO trademark registration 8-12mo before launch → Amazon Brand Registry enrollment → Seller Central 1P-vs-3P decision (3P default for $500k-$5M GMV; 1P recommended for $10M+ GMV) → FBA inbound creation + SKU labeling → listing creation + A+ content + Brand Store → Amazon Sponsored Products + Sponsored Brands launch ($80/day) → Vine review acquisition ($200/SKU + $600-1,500 product cost; 10-20 verified reviews in 30 days) → Buy Box ownership >90% + Amazon DSP branded-keyword defense ($500-2,000/mo via managed-service Tinuiti + Perpetual Traffic + CPC Strategy) → Triple Whale Marketplace Sync + Amazon Attribution + post-purchase email attribution setup (the 3 attribution stitches that prevent Amazon-Halo over-crediting)]; **(b) Phase 2 — Amazon + Walmart (US Amazon 3P+FBA + US Walmart 3P+WFS) ~20 hr cumulative Weeks 5–12** [Walmart Marketplace enrollment (2-4 week approval + NEW listings required) → WFS fulfillment setup ($3-8/unit pick-pack + 2-day shipping badge) → Walmart Sponsored Products + Walmart Connect launch ($45/day; Walmart CPC ~50-70% lower than Amazon per CPC Strategy 2024) → Walmart Buy Box ownership >85% + brand-canary-defense on Walmart (Walmart Brand Registry 4-8 week approval) → Attribution-merge Phase 2 (Triple Whale Walmart sync + Walmart Connect attribution + extended post-purchase email) → Phase 2 verification + steady-state monitoring (Monday morning weekly cadence)]; **(c) Phase 3 — International marketplaces (Amazon EU 5 marketplaces DE+FR+IT+ES+NL + bol NL + Zalando EU + Cdiscount FR + Amazon JP) ~75 hr Weeks 13–24 + 25 hr/wk ongoing** [Amazon EU 5-marketplaces enrollment + Pan-European FBA + EU compliance stack verification (CE + VAT-MOSS + EPR + GPSR effective Dec 2024; $10k-30k one-time + $2k-10k/yr) → bol + Zalando + Cdiscount enrollment + cross-listing automation via Sellbrite/Codisto/LitCommerce ($30-100/mo) → Amazon JP enrollment + JP-language listings + JP-specific compliance (PSE mark + Food Sanitation Act + JP customs) → EU compliance stack audit + GPSR renewal ($1k-5k/yr Responsible-Person appointment)]; **(d) Phase 4 — Target Plus + Walmart International + steady-state ~30 hr Quarter 2+ + dedicated marketplace manager** [Target Plus Roundel vendor application (6-12 month approval + 40-55% wholesale discount + 1P-via-Roundel model) → Walmart International CA + MX enrollment → Steady-state marketplace operations (daily monitoring + weekly review + monthly optimization + quarterly business review across all 14+ marketplaces)]. The playbook ships **the canonical 5 brand-canary-defense levers** (the canonical biggest pitfall per research/06 Pillar 2 + Marketplace Pulse 2024 benchmark): **(1) Amazon Brand Registry** (free; required; unlocks A+ content + Vine + Brand Store + Sponsored Brands + Amazon DSP + Transparency); **(2) Vine review acquisition** ($200/SKU + $600-1,500 product cost; yields 10-20 verified reviews in 30 days vs 90-180 days for organic); **(3) Buy Box >90% ownership** (FBA inventory automatically qualifies; FBM sellers rarely win Buy Box); **(4) Amazon DSP branded-keyword defense** ($500-2,000/mo via managed-service; prevents competitors poaching brand-search-traffic within 30 days of launch); **(5) Amazon Transparency per-unit-serial-codes** ($0.01-0.05/unit; prevents counterfeit + brand-canary-monitoring). The playbook ships **the canonical 5 attribution-merge stitches** (the canonical hard problem per Triple Whale + Amazon Attribution 2024; without these 5 stitches operators underestimate DTC-cannibalization 30-50% and over-credit Amazon-attribution 30-50%): **(1) Amazon Attribution** (free; Amazon-ads attribution to Shopify-conversions + brand-search-lift); **(2) Triple Whale Marketplace Sync** ($200-500/mo Pro add-on; stitches Amazon + Walmart orders into cohort-LTV view); **(3) Post-purchase email** (Klaviyo segment "Marketplace Purchaser (last 30 days)" + 10% off second-purchase-from-our-store coupon); **(4) Amazon Customer Engagement** (free Amazon-owned email channel for re-engagement); **(5) Walmart Connect attribution** ($500-2,000/mo via managed-service Walmart Connect + Tinuiti + Perpetual Traffic). The playbook ships **4 path-tier GMV decision matrix**: Path A — Amazon-only $500k-$5M GMV (1 marketplace, ~25 hr Weeks 1-4, +20-45% incremental net, 8:1 default ROI) / Path B — Amazon + Walmart $1M-$10M GMV DEFAULT (2 marketplaces, ~45 hr Weeks 1-12, +30-70% incremental net, 8.3:1 default ROI at $5M base = $2.25M Year-1 net / $270k cost stack) / Path C — All marketplaces including international $5M-$50M GMV (7+ marketplaces, ~120 hr Weeks 1-24 + 25 hr/wk ongoing, +40-100% incremental net, 10:1 default ROI) / Path D — All marketplaces + Target Plus $10M-$50M GMV (14+ marketplaces, ~150 hr + dedicated marketplace manager, +50-120% incremental net, 12:1 default ROI). The playbook ships **15 numbered pitfalls with corrective `Fix:` lines clustered into 5 failure modes**: A channel-economics errors (Pitfall #1 launch-without-registered-USPTO-trademark → file 8-12mo before via TEAS Plus $250 + Amazon IP Accelerator fallback $1k-5k; #2 default-3P-without-evaluating-1P-vs-3P → run canonical decision matrix research/06 §Pillar 1; #3 ignore-per-marketplace-fee-stack-math → pre-compute per-SKU contribution margin research/06 §Pillar 1 with <30% gate); B brand-canary-protection errors (Pitfall #4 skip-Vine-review-acquisition → enroll hero SKU immediately after Brand Registry approval; #5 lose-Buy-Box-by-switching-FBA-to-FBM → keep hero SKU on FBA + use FBM only for slow-movers ≤10/mo; #6 skip-Amazon-DSP-branded-keyword-defense → allocate $500-2,000/mo via managed-service; #7 Amazon-Halo-effect-not-measured → ship 3 attribution stitches in Phase 1 Step 1.9 + measure DTC-cannibalization-rate monthly; #8 skip-Amazon-Posts → publish 3-5 Posts/week Brand-Registered sellers); C operational-model errors (Pitfall #9 send-slow-movers-to-FBA → send only top-20% velocity SKUs to FBA + auto-deletion 90 days; #10 FBA-inbound-mishaps → use 3PL prep service first 3 shipments; #11 no-returns-management → enroll FBA Grade-and-Resell for hero SKU); D regulatory-friction errors (Pitfall #12 launch-EU-without-CE-VAT-MOSS-EPR-GPSR → complete compliance audit Phase 3 Step 3.4 BEFORE launching EU; #13 launch-gated-category-without-FDA-compliance → consult regulatory attorney $500-2,000/hr + FDA-compliance specialist $2k-10k/SKU; #14 no-per-country-returns-infrastructure → set up global returns partner ReturnGO/Returnly/Loop Returns + local-language return labels); E attribution-measurement errors (Pitfall #15 no-Triple-Whale-Marketplace-Sync + Amazon-Attribution + post-purchase-email-attribution → ship 3 attribution stitches Phase 1 + add Walmart-side Phase 2 + add EU + JP Phase 3). The playbook ships **15-metric monitoring table** + **4 phase-by-phase verification gates with 11/10/10/9 prereqs respectively (40 total)** + **Path B cost-stack line items** ($270,568 median Year-1 cost stack → $2.25M Year-1 incremental net = 8.3:1 median Path B ROI). Compounds research/06 5-pillar framework + Move #1 + Move #4 + Move #6 + Move #8 + Move #11 Phases 1+2 + Asset 13 per-market voice-variant pricing card by mapping each pillar into a step-by-step Amazon Seller Central + Walmart Marketplace + Target Plus + EU marketplaces operator build; the canonical 2nd-layer operator-build companion for the marketplace-expansion track per the research → playbook → asset → operator-surface → scripts → static-dashboard layer order.

The doc ships **the 5-pillar marketplace-expansion framework**: **(a) Pillar 1 — Channel economics** — per-marketplace fee-stack matrix Amazon US 3P 30-45% / Amazon US 1P wholesale-discount / Walmart US 3P 25-35% / Target Plus 1P-via-Roundel 40-55% net-to-brand / Amazon EU 5-marketplace / bol / Zalando / Cdiscount / Amazon JP with referral fee 6-15% + FBA pick-pack $3-7/unit + storage $0.83-2.40/cubic ft/mo + advertising 10-25% + returns 5-15%; Amazon 1P vs 3P vs hybrid decision rule ($10M+ → 1P / $500k-$10M → 3P+FBA / $5M+ complex → hybrid); **(b) Pillar 2 — Brand-canary defense** — the canonical #1 marketplace-expansion pitfall is Amazon Halo (Marketplace Pulse 2024: 10-35% of DTC-direct-organic-search traffic migrates to Amazon post-launch); the protection recipe = 5 levers: Amazon Brand Registry (free; required) + Amazon Vine review-acquisition ($200/SKU + free product) + Buy Box >90% (FBA + competitive-pricing + 99%+ account-health metrics) + Amazon DSP branded-keyword defense ($500-$2k/mo bid on operator's own brand-name) + Amazon Transparency per-unit-serial-codes ($0.01-$0.05/unit); skipping any 1 of the 5 levers bleeds 15-25% DTC-traffic; **(c) Pillar 3 — Operational model** — FBA vs FBM vs SFP vs WFS vs Target Plus decision matrix with FBA fee math ($3.06-$7.35/unit pick-pack by size tier + Q4 storage 3-5× off-peak) + Inventory Performance Index (IPI) >400 healthy + aged-inventory-surcharge >180 days $0.50-$2.50/unit + the canonical 8-12 weeks of expected demand FBA + 4-week backup-3PL FBM-fallback inventory-routing recipe; **(d) Pillar 4 — Category fit + regulatory friction** — 4-tier category-fit matrix (high: apparel + home + beauty + pet + jewelry + consumer-electronics / medium: food + vitamins + supplements + personal-care with FDA-compliance + lot-tracking / low: CBD + alcohol + firearms + medical-devices with Amazon-regulatory-friction / fail: live-plants + aerosols + lithium-batteries-bulk with Amazon-FBA-prohibition) + EU marketplaces regulatory-friction stack (CE marking $2k-$15k + VAT-MOSS $500-$2k setup + EPR $1k-$5k per country + GPSR Responsible-Person $1k-$5k/yr effective Dec 2024 = $10k-$30k one-time + $2k-$10k/yr) — Path C ($5M+ GMV) is the minimum GMV tier for EU marketplace expansion; **(e) Pillar 5 — Attribution merge + DTC-cannibalization measurement** — the canonical hard-problem per Triple Whale + Amazon Attribution 2024; the 3-stitch recipe: Amazon Attribution (free; Amazon-ads attribution to Shopify-conversions + brand-search-lift) + Triple Whale Marketplace Sync (paid; $200-$500/mo stitches Amazon + Walmart orders into cohort-LTV view) + post-purchase email attribution (Klaviyo segment `marketplace_purchaser_30d` + Amazon Customer Engagement tool + Walmart Connect attribution) — without these 3 stitches, operator underestimates DTC-cannibalization 30-50% + over-credits Amazon-attribution 30-50% (the canonical recipe-bias-toward-"Amazon-is-great" trap). The doc ships **3 GMV-tier paths**: **Path A — Amazon-only ($500k-$5M US DTC GMV)** — 1P+3P+Vine+DSP+Posts+Attribution + Triple Whale Marketplace Sync; one-time $5k-$15k + recurring $1k-$3k/mo + 25 hr one-time + 5 hr/wk ongoing; +20-45% incremental net revenue; **8:1 default Year-1 ROI Path A** at $1M base; **Path B — Amazon + Walmart ($1M-$10M US DTC GMV) DEFAULT** — Path A + Walmart 3P + WFS + Walmart Sponsored Products + Walmart Restored; one-time $10k-$25k + recurring $2.2k-$5.2k/mo + 45 hr one-time + 10 hr/wk ongoing; +30-70% incremental net revenue; **12:1 default Year-1 ROI Path B** at $5M base ($2.25M Year-1 incremental / $270k cost = 8.3:1); **Path C — All marketplaces ($5M-$50M US DTC GMV)** — Path B + Amazon EU 5-marketplaces + bol + Zalando + Cdiscount + Amazon JP + Target Plus application + Walmart International CA+MX; one-time $30k-$75k + recurring $7k-$20k/mo + 120 hr one-time + 25 hr/wk ongoing + dedicated marketplace manager; +40-100% incremental net revenue; **10:1 default Year-1 ROI Path C** at $15M base ($9M Year-1 / $400-800k cost). The doc ships **4 phase-by-phase verification gates** with 11/10/10/9 prereqs respectively (Gate A Phase 1 Amazon-only / Gate B Phase 2 Amazon+Walmart / Gate C Phase 3 international / Gate D Phase 4 Target Plus + steady-state), each gating the next phase per the canonical phase-ladder pattern from research/04 + research/05. The doc ships **15 numbered pitfalls with corrective `Fix:` lines** clustered into 5 failure modes: **A channel-economics errors** (Pitfall #1 launch-without-Brand-Registry + #2 3P-vs-1P-default + #3 fee-stack-math-ignored); **B brand-canary-protection errors** (Pitfall #4 skip-Vine + #5 lose-Buy-Box-FBM + #6 skip-Amazon-DSP + #7 Amazon-Halo-not-measured + #8 skip-Amazon-Posts); **C operational-model errors** (Pitfall #9 slow-movers-to-FBA + #10 FBA-inbound-mishaps + #11 no-returns-management); **D regulatory-friction errors** (Pitfall #12 EU-without-CE-VAT-MOSS-EPR-GPSR + #13 gated-category-without-FDA + #14 no-per-country-returns-infrastructure); **E attribution-measurement errors** (Pitfall #15 no-Triple-Whale-Marketplace-Sync+Amazon-Attribution+post-purchase-email). The doc ships **the Cost & ROI estimate** as the canonical line-item table for Path B default $5M GMV brand (Amazon Pro seller $39/mo + FBA pick+pack $42k/yr + FBA storage $15k/yr + Amazon Sponsored Products $60k/yr + Amazon Sponsored Brands $15k/yr + Amazon DSP $15k/yr + Amazon Vine $1k + Walmart WFS $24k/yr + Walmart storage $7.2k/yr + Walmart Sponsored Products $24k/yr + Triple Whale Marketplace Sync $4.2k/yr + operator time $52k/yr = **$270,568 median Year-1 total cost stack** → expected Year-1 incremental net revenue **$2.25M** (45% of $5M base) = **8.3:1 median Path B ROI**). The doc ships **the 5 planned future-tick companions**: `playbooks/13-marketplace-launch.md` (operator-build companion for Amazon 1P-vs-3P + Brand Registry + listing-creation + Walmart-onboarding + Target-Plus-application + EU-onboarding + attribution-merge setup; ~2 hr) + `assets/15-marketplace-listing-card.md` (paste-ready per-marketplace per-category listing card with title-template + bullet-point-template + A+-content-skeleton + per-voice per-marketplace description variant + keyword-stuffing guardrail; ~2 hr) + `scripts/marketplace_unit_economics.py` (Archetype A/B hybrid Path A/B/C scorer taking US GMV + category + AOV + margin + Amazon-fulfillment-mode + brand-registry-status → outputs Path recommendation + cost-stack + Year-1 incremental revenue + DTC-cannibalization-adjusted net lift + 6-step build; ~1.5 hr) + `dashboards/marketplace-expansion-health.html` (static HTML dashboard rendering per-marketplace launch readiness + per-marketplace revenue contribution + 4-phase gate status + DTC-cannibalization overlay; ~1.5 hr) + `dashboard/app/marketplace/page.tsx` (Next.js operator-surface route; ~45 min). Renders **6 sections end-to-end** that visualize all 5 prior lifecycle-marketing artifacts as a 1-click launch-readiness heat-map against the canonical 78 gate-flow combinations: **(1) Launch-ladder progress** — 6 stat cards (Path tier / 95:1 default Year-1 ROI / live flows 13/17 / Tier 1 launch 5/5 / Tier 2 launch 5/5 / Tier 3+4 launch 3/7) sourced from research/05 §TL;DR + playbook 12 §4-tier launch ladder. **(2) Per-pillar readiness** — 5 pillar cards (P1 Browse-abandon + consideration / P2 Winback + sunset / P3 Post-purchase + loyalty / P4 Replenishment / P5 Lifecycle celebratory) each with status pill (LIVE / DRAFT / STAGING / NOT-STARTED) + live flow count + per-pillar revenue-per-1k floor ($300-800 / $400-1.2k / $500-1.5k / $800-2.5k / $200-800 from research/05 §Pillar canonical KPI tables). **(3) Per-tier revenue contribution bar chart** — 4 bars (Tier 1 / Tier 2 / Tier 3 / Tier 4) each with Path A/B/C revenue share (sourced from research/05 §TL;DR: Tier 1 28:1 default ROI / Tier 2 18:1 / Tier 3 12:1 / Tier 4 6:1; Path B weights 45/30/15/10 sum to 100%). Pure CSS bar chart (`<div class="bar-fill" style="width: 35%"></div>`) — no Chart.js. **(4) Per-pillar 6-gate verification scoring** — 5 cards (one per pillar) each scoring the pillar's live flows against the canonical 6-gate benchmark (Gate A open_rate ≥35% / Gate B click_rate ≥4% / Gate C CVR ≥0.8% / Gate D unsub_rate ≤0.3% / Gate E revenue_per_1k ≥ per-pillar floor / Gate F flow_attribution_match ≥60% Triple Whale signal) per `scripts/lifecycle_flow_health_check.py`. **(5) Per-flow detail table** — 17 rows × 6 columns (Flow ID / Flow name / Pillar / Tier / Channel / Status / Verdict / Gates passed / Open-Click-CVR) covering all 17 documented flows with their canonical IDs matching the script's PATH_B_FLOWS schema (`1.1_browse_abandon` / `2.1_birthday` / `3.4_account_never_purchased` / etc.). **(6) Recommended next action** — context-aware ordered list (Tier 1 launch state + Tier 2 launch state + audit invocation guidance + Triple Whale integration reminder + Path ROI baseline). **4 canonical data structures** (sourced verbatim from research/05 + scripts/lifecycle_flow_health_check.py): **FLOWS** (17 documented flows × 5 pillars × 4 tiers × {channel, expected_roi, sms}); **PILLARS** (5 pillars × canonical per-pillar revenue-per-1k floor + name + flow_count + gate_score_default); **TIER_TABLE** (4 tiers × {label, roi, pathA_share, pathB_share, pathC_share, default_roi}); **GATES** (6 canonical KPI gates with floor + ok/warn/fail CSS class). **8 helper functions** (`pathForGMV` / `tierForFlow` / `statusClass` / `statusLabel` / `verdictForFlow` / `fmtUSD` / `fmtPct` / `verdictClass`) — the canonical 8-helpers-per-static-dashboard pattern from the international-expansion-health dashboard (v0.11.0 static-dashboard-tick recipe). **6 render functions** (`renderSummary` / `renderPillarGrid` / `renderTierChart` / `renderGateGrid` / `renderFlowsTable` / `renderNextAction`). **4 URL params** (canonical pattern from sibling dashboards): `?path=A | B | C` (override path tier) / `?us_gmv=<number>` (US GMV in dollars; default $5M for Path B) / `?input=<json-url>` (fetch JSON payload with AbortController + 1500ms timeout; falls back to SAMPLE_INPUTS on timeout/error) / `?demo=1` (force demo mode). **fetch-timeout contract** (canonical 1500ms per the v0.11.0 static-dashboard-tick recipe): `AbortController` + `setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), FETCH_TIMEOUT_MS)` + `clearTimeout` in `finally` block. Demo mode shows the canonical Path B default (13 Path-B live flows out of 17 documented; 5 Tier 1 + 5 Tier 2 + 3 Tier 3 subset live; 4 Tier 3-or-4 documented in DRAFT). **`dashboards/tests/test_lifecycle_flow_library.js`** (new, 100-test Node smoke suite across 18 categories: HTML structure [5] + script parse [1] + 6 UI sections present [6] + fetch-timeout contract [4] + URL param parsing [3] + FLOWS array shape with 17 documented flows + tier distribution T1/T2/T3/T4 sums to 17 [5] + PILLARS object with 5 pillars + per-pillar revenue floors $300-800/$400-1200/$500-1500/$800-2500/$200-800 [10] + TIER_TABLE with 4 tiers + Path B shares 45/30/15/10 sum to 100% + per-tier default ROI 28/18/12/6 [8] + GATES array with 6 canonical gates + per-gate floor [12] + SAMPLE_INPUTS Path B $5M + 13 live + 4 draft + per-flow status assertions [9] + 6 rendering functions present [6] + 8 helper functions present [8] + pathForGMV classifier with $1M/$10M thresholds [5] + verdictForFlow 6-gate scoring with PASS/WARN/NEEDS_WORK/FAIL bands [9] + 5 companion artifact references [5] + vm-sandbox demo-mode render [1] + no anti-pattern grep [1] + file size ≤60KB [1] = **100 tests total**). Pure-Node smoke suite (no jsdom dep); mirrors the v0.11.0 17-category Node smoke suite pattern from the international-expansion-health dashboard (71 tests) + the unified-attribution-health dashboard (59 tests); each test is a single regex/structural assertion.

The lifecycle-marketing track is now **fully complete across all 6 canonical layers** — research 6/6 + playbooks 17/17 + scripts 13/13 + dashboards 2→3 + assets 14/14 + Next.js route /lifecycle (shipped 2026-06-28 as the 4th layer) BEFORE this tick; the static-dashboard layer was the canonical 6th-and-final layer. **Compounds 5 prior artifacts in 1 bounded tick:** (i) **research/05 §20-flow library** — the FLOWS array's 17 entries match the canonical 4-tier × 5-pillar scope (Tier 1: 5 / Tier 2: 5 / Tier 3: 4 / Tier 4: 3) with canonical flow IDs matching scripts/lifecycle_flow_health_check.py `PATH_B_FLOWS` schema; (ii) **playbook 12 §Step-by-step 4-tier launch ladder** — the dashboard's per-tier launch-progress cards (Tier 1 5/5 / Tier 2 5/5 / Tier 3+4 3/7) mirror the canonical playbook 12 ship-cadence (Tier 1 Week 1 / Tier 2 Days 8-30 / Tier 3 Days 31-90 / Tier 4 Quarter 2+); (iii) **asset 14 §85 voice-variant templates** — the per-flow detail table surfaces the 17 flows that the asset 14 templates ship for; the voice-driven override columns in asset 14 are visualized via the dashboard's per-pillar readiness cards (5 pillars × 17 flows × {live/draft/staging}); (iv) **`scripts/lifecycle_flow_health_check.py` §6-gate scoring** — the dashboard's Gate A/B/C/D/E/F scoring per pillar mirrors the script's 78 gate-flow combinations (6 gates × 13 Path-B live flows) using the canonical thresholds (open ≥35% / click ≥4% / CVR ≥0.8% / unsub ≤0.3% / revenue_per_1k ≥ pillar floor / attribution ≥60%); (v) **/lifecycle Next.js route (4th layer)** — the static dashboard is the canonical SIBLING surface to the Next.js route, surfacing the same 5 prior artifacts but as a self-contained portable HTML file that operators can email / archive in Dropbox / run offline (the Next.js route requires `npx next dev` on port 8767; the static dashboard serves from any `python3 -m http.server` with zero install). **The 78 gate-flow combinations** is the canonical scope number research/05 line 287 forward-points ("6 gates × 13 flows = 78 gate-flow combinations"); the dashboard's KPI thresholds are pinned as module constants in scripts/lifecycle_flow_health_check.py + mirrored in the dashboard's GATES array so a future contributor cannot silently loosen them without modifying both files. **The 17 documented flow IDs match the script's canonical PATH_B_FLOWS schema** (`1.1_browse_abandon` / `1.2_winback` / ... / `4.3_seasonal_gift_guide`) for operator traceability — operators running `python3 scripts/lifecycle_flow_health_check.py --bootstrap --fixtures-dir ./lifecycle_fixtures/` will see the same flow IDs in the fixture JSON that the dashboard renders as the per-flow table rows. **Honest-read called out in 4 places:** (a) **The dashboard's SAMPLE_INPUTS uses 13 Path-B live flows** (5 Tier 1 + 5 Tier 2 + 3 Tier 3 subset) per research/05 line 287 — the 4 additional documented flows (stock-back Tier 3 + 3 Tier 4 quarterly) are surfaced as DRAFT; operators running Tier 3 replenishment / Tier 4 quarterly flows should NOT see those rows as live until they ship them per playbook 12 §Step-by-step cadence. (b) **The dashboard's per-flow demo data is SYNTHETIC** — every open_rate / click_rate / CVR / revenue_per_1k value is sourced from research/05 §Pillar canonical KPI benchmarks (e.g. P1 Browse-abandon $300-800/1k events; P2 Winback $400-1.2k/1k; P3 Post-purchase $500-1.5k/1k) + Klaviyo 2024 lifecycle-benchmark ranges; operators with real per-flow KPI data should override via `?input=<json-url>` URL param with their own JSON payload (the AbortController + 1500ms fetch-timeout fallback ensures the dashboard always renders even when the URL is offline). (c) **The dashboard is gated on ≥30 days of live flow data** — research/05 line 287 + playbook 12 §Companion tool explicitly state "gated on the 20 flows being live for ≥30 days before the script can score them"; rendering the dashboard against a flow that's been live <30 days produces noisy PASS/WARN/NEEDS_WORK verdicts due to insufficient statistical power (a flow with 200 sends hasn't accumulated enough signal to reliably tell PASS from WARN). (d) **The dashboard does NOT score seasonal flows well** — birthday + anniversary + seasonal-gift-guide have highly variable monthly send volumes (expect 1/12 of list per day for birthday, 0 sends most days for anniversary outside the customer's anniversary month); the per-pillar revenue floor for P5 Lifecycle celebratory ($200-800) is intentionally LOWER than P1-P4 to account for the lower send volume, but operators running these flows at small list size (<500 anniversary-eligible customers) will see false-FAIL verdicts due to insufficient statistical power — the canonical fix is to defer scoring until the flow has ≥500 sends in the trailing 30 days.

## [2026-06-28 11:30] Script track — `scripts/lifecycle_flow_health_check.py` (Archetype C/D-light hybrid per-flow KPI audit; 6 canonical gates × 13 Path-B live flows = 78 gate-flow combinations; the canonical 5th layer of the lifecycle-marketing track per the research → playbook → asset → operator-surface → scripts layer order; the canonical script-tick follow-up to the 2026-06-28 05:30 `/lifecycle` route tick per the prior-tick's next-action recommendation + count-dominance + layer-order-completion + pick-signal convergence [all 3 signals agreed on this script])

- **What shipped:** `scripts/lifecycle_flow_health_check.py` (new, ~530 lines / 20KB / the 13th script in the workspace + the **canonical script-track follow-up to research/05 + playbook 12 + asset 14 + the /lifecycle route** per the canonical 6-layer extended layer order research → playbook → asset → operator-surface → script → static-dashboard). Archetype C/D-light hybrid per-flow KPI audit that takes one JSON fixture per live flow (kpis_30d: sent / opens / clicks / conversions / unsubscribes / revenue / flow_attributed) and scores each flow against the canonical 6-gate benchmark matrix: **Gate A** open_rate ≥ 35% (Klaviyo 2024 floor) / **Gate B** click_rate ≥ 4% (Klaviyo 2024 floor) / **Gate C** CVR ≥ 0.8% (Klaviyo 2024 floor) / **Gate D** unsubscribe_rate ≤ 0.3% (deliverability ceiling per Klaviyo + Postscript) / **Gate E** revenue_per_1k ≥ per-pillar floor (P1 Browse-abandon $300-800 / P2 Winback-sunset $400-1,200 / P3 Post-purchase-loyalty $500-1,500 / P4 Replenishment $800-2,500 / P5 Celebratory $200-800 — all from research/05 §Pillar canonical KPI tables) / **Gate F** flow_attribution_match ≥ 60% (Triple Whale cohort-sync signal per playbook 12 §Step 2.4). Each flow gets a 0–100 overall_score + a per-gate pass/fail tally + a prioritized fix-list of the failed gates with the measured value + the canonical floor + the corrective action. 4 verdict levels: PASS (≥90 score, all 6 gates pass) / WARN (75-89, 5 gates pass) / NEEDS_WORK (50-74, 3-4 gates pass) / FAIL (<50, ≤2 gates pass). 6 canonical pillars + 13 Path-B live flows = **78 gate-flow combinations** per research/05 line 287 (the canonical scope number the playbook scopes). The script is **hermetic** — no Klaviyo / Postscript / Smile / Triple Whale API access required; operator-supplied JSON fixtures + local scoring rule. Mirrors the canonical Archetype C/D-light hybrid pattern from Move #6.5 + #6.6 + #6.7 (the 3 attribution-quality-audit scripts that ship the same JSON-fixture-based numeric-threshold audit shape). `--bootstrap` writes 13 canonical-pass fixtures (one per Path-B live flow: 5 Tier-1 + 5 Tier-2 + 3 Tier-3 subset = browse-abandon + winback + post-purchase cross-sell + sunset + shipping/transit + birthday + anniversary + loyalty tier-up/tier-down + NPS-detractor + subscription renewal+dunning + VIP early-access + replenishment + account-never-purchased) with per-pillar-revenue-floor-target values that all pass the canonical 6 gates. `--only-check <flow_id>` returns 0 if that flow PASSes/WARNs; 1 if it NEEDS_WORK/FAILs (for ad-hoc per-flow audits + cron alert wiring). `--json` emits a clean JSON output (top-level keys: fixture_dir / overall {passed, summary {total, by_pillar, by_tier, PASS/WARN/NEEDS_WORK/FAIL counts}} / scores [{flow_id, flow_name, pillar, tier, channel, verdict, overall_score, gates_passed, gates_failed, failed_gates, open_rate, click_rate, cvr, unsubscribe_rate, revenue_per_1k, flow_attribution_match}, ...]) for cron / CI / dashboard piping. Exits 0 if all flows PASS/WARN; exits 1 if any flow NEEDS_WORK/FAIL (for Slack alert wiring).

- **Why this move:** Per the prior tick (2026-06-28 05:30 `/lifecycle` route tick)'s explicit next-action recommendation: **(i) `scripts/lifecycle_flow_health_check.py`** → **(ii) `dashboards/lifecycle-flow-library.html`**. **Pre-staging count is 4 distinct artifacts** (research/05 lines 292 + 352 + playbook 12 lines 7 + 527 + 534 + asset 14 lines 7 + 390 + 491 + research/03 line 179 — exactly the 2+ pre-staging threshold for the canonical pick × multiple-artifacts). **The cron-template signal AND the 4-artifact pre-staging signal AND the v0.9.0 layer-order-completion sub-rule AND the v0.10.0 pick-signal convergence pattern all AGREE on `scripts/lifecycle_flow_health_check.py`** — 4 signals converging on a single candidate is the strongest possible pick per the cron-driven-bounded-improver recipe. The script track was the **canonical next layer** per the research → playbook → asset → operator-surface-route → **script** layer order (research/05 + playbook 12 + asset 14 + /lifecycle route all shipped; the script was the canonical 5th layer to close the lifecycle-marketing track). **The script track was the thinnest remaining layer after the route shipped** — research 6/6 complete + playbooks 17/17 complete (top-10 + 5 attribution-quality + 1 international + 1 lifecycle) + scripts 12/12 complete (4 attribution-quality + 3 KPI-ROI + 1 international + 4 attribution-quality follow-ons + 2 audit + 2 scoring) + dashboards 2/2 complete + assets 14/14 complete BEFORE this tick; the only remaining forward-pointer with 4+ pre-staging signal was `scripts/lifecycle_flow_health_check.py`. **The script compounds 4 prior artifacts**: research/05 §Pillar canonical KPI tables (the 5 per-pillar revenue floors P1-P5: $300-800 / $400-1.2k / $500-1.5k / $800-2.5k / $200-800 are pulled directly from the research doc's per-Pillar canonical-KPI sections) + playbook 12 §Step-by-step expected lift bands (the canonical Tier 1+2+3 expected-lift targets per Step 1.1-3.4 are the script's per-flow comparison baseline) + asset 14 §Suppression rules (the 11 suppression rules across the 17 flows are the canonical per-flow "who-should-not-receive-this-flow" filters the script's audience-correctness gate could later extend) + Move #6 Triple Whale cohort-sync signal (the Gate F flow_attribution_match ≥60% floor mirrors Move #6's Klaviyo-Triple Whale integration benchmark per playbook 12 §Step 2.4). **The 6 canonical gates × 13 Path-B live flows = 78 gate-flow combinations** is the canonical scope number research/05 line 287 forward-points ("6 gates × 13 flows = 78 gate-flow combinations"); the script's KPI thresholds are pinned as module constants (`OPEN_RATE_FLOOR = 0.35` / `CLICK_RATE_FLOOR = 0.04` / `CVR_FLOOR = 0.008` / `UNSUBSCRIBE_RATE_CEIL = 0.003` / `FLOW_ATTRIBUTION_MATCH_FLOOR = 0.60` / `REVENUE_FLOORS_PER_PILLAR` dict of 5 pillar-specific `(low, high)` tuples) so a future contributor cannot silently loosen them without modifying the module-level constants AND the matching `test_canonical_thresholds_published` test that asserts every threshold value. **Honest-read called out in 4 places:** (a) **Gate F attribution floor is intentionally stricter than Move #6's 50% benchmark** — research/05 §Pillar 5 sets the lifecycle-attribution floor at 60% (vs Move #6's overall 50% for the attribution-quality-audit scripts) because lifecycle flows have clearer attribution signal than the attribution-quality audits (lifecycle flows are tied to specific Klaviyo flow_ids via the `?tw_camp=<flow_id>` UTM, so a 60% match is achievable in steady state); operators with weaker Triple Whale-Klaviyo integration will trip Gate F first and need to wire the integration per playbook 12 §Step 2.4 before the script becomes useful. (b) **The script is gated on ≥30 days of live flow data** — research/05 line 287 + playbook 12 §Companion tool explicitly state "gated on the 20 flows being live for ≥30 days before the script can score them"; running the script on a flow that's been live <30 days produces noisy signals (a flow with 200 sends hasn't accumulated enough statistical power to reliably tell PASS from WARN). (c) **The 13 Path-B live flows in `PATH_B_FLOWS` are the canonical $500k-$10M GMV Path-B subset** (5 Tier-1 + 5 Tier-2 + 3 Tier-3 subset); Path A operators (Tier-1-only, 5 flows) and Path C operators (all 4 tiers, 20 flows) would need different `PATH_*_FLOWS` tables — the script supports `--fixtures-dir <path>` to override, so the operator can ship their own `path_a_fixtures/` or `path_c_fixtures/` with the appropriate flow IDs + pillars without modifying the module. (d) **The script does NOT score seasonal flows well** — birthday + anniversary + seasonal-gift-guide have highly variable monthly send volumes (expect 1/12 of list per day for birthday, 0 sends most days for anniversary outside the customer's anniversary month); the per-pillar revenue floor for P5 celebratory ($200-800) is intentionally LOWER than P1-P4 to account for the lower send volume, but operators running these flows at small list size (<500 anniversary-eligible customers) will see false-FAIL verdicts due to insufficient statistical power — the canonical fix is to defer scoring until the flow has ≥500 sends in the trailing 30 days.

- **What shipped:** `scripts/international_market_fit.py` (490 lines / 23KB / the **12th script** in the workspace + the canonical Archetype A/B hybrid scoring script for the international-expansion track + the **script-layer completion** of the research → playbook → asset → operator-surface → scripts canonical layer order for the international trio) + `scripts/tests/test_international_market_fit.py` (340 lines / 16KB / 25 TDD tests across 1 test class — the matching test file per the canonical script-tick recipe). The script takes a brand's US-baseline inputs (US GMV / category / AOV / contribution margin / supply-chain complexity / operator capacity) and outputs a **Path A / B / C / C+ recommendation** with cost stack + expected Year-1 lift + per-market projection + 6-step build sequence. The script ships **6 input dimensions + 4-tier path output + 3 downgrade gates + 12-category tier classification**: (a) **BrandInputs dataclass** with 6 fields validated in `__post_init__` (us_gmv ≥ 0 / us_aov > 0 / contribution margin 0–100 / supply-chain complexity ∈ {1,2,3} / operator capacity ≥ 0 / category ∈ 12 supported values + "other" fallback). (b) **`classify_category()`** returns high / medium / low fit per research/00 §Pillar 1 (apparel + beauty + home_goods = high; electronics + jewelry + pet = medium; food + supplements + cbd + alcohol + firearms + medical_devices = low; unknown = medium conservative default). (c) **`recommend_path()`** applies the canonical scoring rule from research/04 §GMV-tier paths + playbook 11 §Prerequisites: **path-tier floor rule** (US GMV < $1M → Path A as deferral; $1M–$10M → Path B default; $10M–$50M → Path C; > $50M → Path C+ with in-region 3PL) + **3 downgrade gates** applied cumulatively (contribution margin < 30% gate per playbook 11 §Prerequisite #6 → downgrade one tier; supply-chain complexity = 3 → downgrade one tier; operator capacity < 4 hr/wk → downgrade one tier per playbook 11 §Prerequisite #8). (d) **`project_per_market_lift()`** emits per-market Year-1 revenue projection using the path-specific market-share weights (Path A: CA 100% / Path B: CA 35% + UK 30% + EU 25% + AU 10% / Path C: CA 20% + UK 18% + EU 16% + AU 10% + JP 14% + DACH 12% + Nordics 10% — sums to 100% per path; sourced from research/04 + asset 13). (e) **`build_sequence_for_path()`** returns the 6-step build recipe from asset 13 §6-step build (Path A: 30 min/1 hr/45 min/1 hr/skip/45 min = ~3.75 hr bounded; Path B: 30 min/1 hr/45 min/1 hr/30 min/45 min = ~4.25 hr; Path C: 30 min/2 hr/2 hr/1 hr/1 hr/1 hr/wk = ~7.25 hr one-time + 1 hr/wk recurring; Path C+: 1 hr/3 hr/3 hr/2 hr/2 hr/2 hr/wk = ~13 hr one-time + 2 hr/wk recurring). (f) **`render_human()` + `main()`** for the human-readable + `--json` CLI output modes (the JSON output includes the inputs + recommendation + per-market projection nested objects, ready for dashboard piping or cron/CI consumption). The default inputs mirror the canonical research/04 + playbook 11 Path B reference ($5M US GMV apparel brand at $75 AOV with 70% margin and 8 hr/wk operator capacity) so the bare `python3 international_market_fit.py` command surfaces the canonical "Path B default" output that an operator can read and trust without any CLI flags.

(d) **downgrade gates are cumulative** — if all 3 gates fail (margin < 30% AND supply chain = 3 AND operator < 4 hr/wk), the path downgrades from base by 3 tiers (not 1); a $5M brand with all gates failing drops from Path B → Path A as deferral (correct — these 3 gates are precisely the reasons NOT to launch). (2) **Decision matrix — which path fits your brand + which markets ship first** — 3-path GMV-tier decision matrix (Path A <$500k US GMV → CA only, 1-market × 5-voice = 5 cells; Path B $1M–$10M US GMV → CA + UK + EU + AU default, 4 markets × 5 voices = 20 cells with JP/DACH/Nordics pre-staged as drafts; Path C $10M–$50M US GMV → all 7 markets, 7 × 5 = 35 cells fully launched). The playbook maps research/04's 5-pillar framework (Market selection + Currency/FX + Duties/Taxes + Fulfillment + Localization) into a **3-phase, 6-phase-build, 4-phase-gate rollout** over **6–12 months**. The playbook ships **14 top-level sections**: (1) **Goal** — frame the 6 deliverables (live cross-border storefront + tax/duty compliance + 3PL cross-border fulfillment + localized payment methods + voice framework localization + per-market ad campaigns). (2) **Which path fits your brand** — 3-path GMV-tier decision matrix (Path A <$500k US GMV → CA only, $300–$500/mo cost stack, 10–25% lift, 15:1 to 40:1 ROI; Path B $1M–$10M US GMV → Phase 1+2 default = CA + UK + EU + AU, $800–$1,500/mo cost stack, **30–80% lift, 20:1 to 60:1 ROI (25:1 median)**; Path C $10M–$50M US GMV → all 7 markets + in-region 3PL, $1,500–$2,500/mo cost stack, 50–150% lift, 30:1 to 100:1 ROI). (3) **Prerequisites** — 12-prereq gate (US Shopify store + 12mo order history + baseline unit-econ / admin access to Shopify + Meta + Google + Klaviyo + 3PL / ≥30% US contribution margin / Asset 02 voice framework / retention stack Move #1+#4+#7+#8 / Triple Whale Move #6 / 4–8 hr/wk + $5k–$25k setup / cross-border-friendly product / 3PL cross-border rate quotes / IOSS registration / UK VAT MOSS registration / GDPR-compliant email capture). (4) **Phase 1 — Canada + UK (Months 1–2)** — 5-step build (Step 1.1 activate Shopify Markets + Markets PRO for DDP duties automation / Step 1.2 wire 3PL cross-border rates into Shopify Shipping / Step 1.3 IOSS + UK VAT MOSS registration in parallel / Step 1.4 localize Default voice to UK-English via `assets/02b-brand-voice-uk.md` / Step 1.5 launch + monitor 30 days against Phase 1 Gate A). (5) **Phase 2 — EU + Australia (Months 3–5)** — 4-step build (Step 2.1 activate EU + AU markets + DE/FR/ES localization / Step 2.2 wire translation + voice localization for EU per **EU Green Claims Directive 2026** / Step 2.3 add Klarna + AfterPay payment methods for DACH/Nordics + AU BNPL lift 30–50% CVR / Step 2.4 launch + monitor 60 days against Phase 2 Gate B). (6) **Phase 3 — Japan + DACH + Nordics (Months 6–12, optional for Path B; required for Path C)** — 2-step build (Step 3.1 activate JP + DACH + Nordics + in-region 3PL EU warehouse + JP warehouse + Konbini payment for JP / Step 3.2 launch + monitor 90 days against Phase 3 Gate C). (7) **Phase 4 — Steady-state international ops** — 4 ongoing cadences (weekly Triple Whale per-market cohort review / monthly Klaviyo per-locale flow review / quarterly per-market pricing re-baseline / annual market-expansion re-evaluation to BR + MX + IN + KR + SG). (8) **Metrics to track** — 12-row per-market monitoring table (per-market revenue / CVR / AOV / CAC payback / LTV:CAC / per-locale flow CVR / per-locale unsub rate / FX fee % / DDP duty cost % / Klarna+AfterPay BNPL share / Konbini share / GDPR-compliant email capture rate). (9) **Common pitfalls** — **15 numbered pitfalls with corrective `Fix:` lines** mapping each failure mode to the canonical fix (Launching EU without IOSS → Apply for IOSS in Phase 1 Day 3–7 / Using US prices currency-converted → Apply per-market pricing premium / Not localizing voice for UK English → Create `assets/02b-brand-voice-uk.md` / Forgetting UK is no longer in EU → UK has its own VAT MOSS / Shipping from US with 14-day delivery → Set 7–14 day expectations in PDP + checkout / Not setting up Klarna/AfterPay in DACH → Wire BNPL in Step 2.3 / Charging duties on delivery without warning → Use DDP / Not budgeting FX fees → Track 1.5–3.5% / Returning US-sized packaging internationally → Audit packaging size / Using US-only returns policy → Localize per market / Translating with Google Translate only → Use DeepL + native-speaker review / Not adapting Klaviyo flows to local time zones → Per-locale send-time optimization / Launching JP without Konbini → Wire Konbini in Step 3.1 / Forgetting GDPR for EU email capture → Klaviyo double opt-in + GDPR form / Scaling international before US unit economics work → US contribution margin ≥30% prerequisite). (10) **Verification gates** — 4 phase-by-phase gates (Gate A Phase 1 Day 30: 10 sub-gates A1-A10 / Gate B Phase 2 Day 60: 11 sub-gates B1-B11 / Gate C Phase 3 Day 90: 10 sub-gates C1-C10 / Gate D steady-state monthly: 9 sub-gates D1-D9). (11) **Cost & ROI estimate** — 3-tier table (Path A: $500–$2,000 one-time + $300–$500/mo recurring → 15:1 to 40:1 ROI / **Path B: $2,500–$7,500 one-time + $600–$1,200/mo recurring → 20:1 to 60:1 conservative default ratio, 25:1 median** / Path C: $15k–$30k one-time + $1,500–$2,500/mo recurring → 30:1 to 100:1 ROI). (12) **Companion tool** — `scripts/triple_whale_attribution_check.py` (Move #6) is the prerequisite for per-market attribution quality; a future-tick companion `scripts/international_attribution_check.py` is planned for per-market sub-reports. - **What shipped:** `assets/11-cs-training-program.md` (~500 lines / 68KB / the eleventh artifact in the `assets/` track — a paste-ready CS-rep onboarding training program that closes the **post-purchase voice-adoption gap** that Asset 08's 12-scenario library makes visible. Asset 08 ships the durable artifact (56 templates × 5 voice profiles); but templates alone don't shape customer outcomes — **CS reps do**. A library that sits unused is 0% leveraged; a library that reps misapply (the mis-toned-Luxury-response trap from Asset 08 Pitfall #1) is actively harmful. Asset 11 IS the training program that ensures the library is actually USED by CS reps with the right tone. Per Asset 02's voice framework, **every module teaches the 5 voice-driven override columns** (Default + Luxury + Sustainable + Gen-Z + B2B) and the 5-voice selection heuristic (Move #8 tier → Klaviyo segment → order history → default fallback, a <30-second decision flow). The framework ships **10 top-level sections** mirroring Asset 09 + Asset 10's canonical 8-section skeleton + 1 measurement-gates section + 1 4-week-ramp-curriculum section: (1) **Goal** — frames why CS-rep training is the adoption layer for Asset 08's library, not a replacement; Asset 08 + Asset 11 together raise template adoption from 30–50% (Asset 08 alone) to 80–95% + measurably higher CSAT + NPS-detractor recovery; **6 honest-read callouts** (training is the adoption layer / 4-week ramp is canonical for 3–10 reps; longer for >10 reps / solo operators can ship Week 1+2 in 2 weeks / the 5 voice-driven override profile cards are the single highest-leverage training artifact / CS-rep measurement is the leading indicator of churn per Asset 05 / the 5 measurement gates are gating, not aspirational). (2) **Decision matrix — which modules to ship first + which reps to train first** — 12 training modules 1:1 with Asset 08's 12 scenarios + rep-staffing decision matrix (1–3 reps / 4–10 reps / 11–30 reps / 30+ reps each get a different training approach + timeline + external-trainer recommendation). Week 1 ships Modules 1/2/3/4/11 (WISMO + shipping-delay + wrong-size + defective + discount-code = ~55–75% CS volume) + Gorgias fluency drill + 5-voice override profile cards. Week 2 ships Modules 5/6/7 (refund + NPS-detractor + loyalty-tier) + Klaviyo NPS-detractor routing drill (higher bar 90% passing). Week 3 ships Modules 8/9/10 (UGC-creator + B2B-AM + subscription). Week 4 ships Module 12 (general-inquiry) + measurement module + continuous-improvement module. (3) **The 12 training modules (paste-ready curriculum)** — 60 module/scenario pairings (12 modules × 5 voice profiles = 60 — though Module 11 discount-code is tone-neutral so ships 5 voice variants not 5 module-voice overrides). Each module ships 6 elements: 1) Reading list (Asset 08 scenario + Asset 02 voice section + supporting research, 30–60 min) / 2) 5-voice override matrix (concrete before/after template pairings per voice) / 3) 5-voice selection heuristic (the <30-second decision flow) / 4) Drill (10–15 multiple-choice + role-play scenarios, 30–90 min) / 5) Anti-pattern red flags (3–5 per module) / 6) Measurement tie-in (how the rep's work shows up in Asset 05 cohort-LTV). **Module 1 WISMO** (2 hours) — tone-neutral across all voices; the only variation is greeting + signoff; Gorgias Automate deflection target ≥30% per Gorgias benchmark. **Module 2 shipping-delay** (3 hours) — apology-tone varies by voice (Default "I'm really sorry" / Luxury "We deeply regret" + concierge follow-up / Sustainable "every shipment matters" + mission framing / Gen-Z "i am SO sorry 😩" / B2B "operational impact" + AM-led follow-up). **Module 3 wrong-size** (3 hours) — prepaid-return-label is non-negotiable per Asset 08 Scenario 3; 70–80% exchange completion with prepaid label vs 30–50% without. **Module 4 defective** (4 hours) — the highest-LTV-recovery scenario per Asset 05 Metric #5 RPR; photo-evidence collection drill + 90% passing score on the photo drill; mis-toned defective responses see 20–35% 90-day-RPR vs 60–80% for nailed-tone. **Module 5 refund** (3 hours) — paired with Move #8 points-deduct rule; refund within 24 hours is gating (5–10 day delay = top-decile churn trigger). **Module 6 NPS-detractor** (4 hours, higher bar 90% passing) — 48-hour SLA is the canonical "we care" signal; 5+ day delay = 90-day churn; Klaviyo NPS-detractor routing drill is the canonical Asset 06 Q7-yes inbound. **Module 7 loyalty-tier** (3 hours) — Move #8 tier-up is celebratory; points-balance framing differs by voice (Sustainable = "X kg of carbon-offset" not "1,200 points"). **Module 8 UGC-creator** (4 hours) — Asset 03 C1/C2/C3 contract-type drill + Asset 10 Dimension 5 FTC-disclosure language; Sustainable + B2B lean gifting + impact-aligned affiliate; Luxury = `#partner` not `#sponsored` per Asset 10. **Module 9 B2B-AM** (4 hours) — single-voice scenario (B2B-formal); AM-coordination is gating. **Module 10 subscription** (3 hours) — "pause vs cancel" alternative is the canonical retention move; 35–50% 30-day-resume rate per Move #11. **Module 11 discount-code** (2 hours) — tone-neutral; Gorgias Automate deflection target 30–60%. **Module 12 general-inquiry** (2 hours, lower bar 70%) — first-impression brand-voice application; the #1 cause of "I never heard back" NPS-Passive bucket per Gorgias benchmark. (4) **The 5 voice-driven override profile cards (laminated at every CS workstation)** — the single highest-leverage training artifact per Gorgias benchmark; reduces voice-mis-application from 25–40% to 5–10% within 30 days. Each card ships 5 elements: 1) 3 tone tells (use) / 2) 3 tone tells (avoid) / 3) 3 customer signals (when to use this voice) / 4) 3 sample template pairings (Default → override) / 5) 2 anti-pattern red flags. **Default** (Hi / Thanks / "no worries" / "lmk" / mid-formality / light humor — avoid: "Dearest" Luxury / emoji Gen-Z / mission Sustainable / formal B2B). **Luxury** (Dearest / "We deeply regret" / concierge / "With warm regards" / complimentary / no humor / hand-written-card — avoid: "OMG" / emoji / "no worries" / casual / mission-framing — anti-pattern: 80% of Luxury CX failures come from mis-toned responses per Asset 06 Q8). **Sustainable** (Hi + 🌱 / mission-first / "carbon-offset" / "every shipment matters" / mid-formality — avoid: "OMG" / "Dearest" / "no worries" / "complimentary"). **Gen-Z** (omg / lol / 💛 / ✨ / lmk / ty / 🎉 / easy! / no stress / low-formality / high-humor / emoji-heavy / lowercase — avoid: "Dearest" / "We deeply regret" / concierge / mission / formal). **B2B** (Dear + account-name / "We sincerely" / "Regards" / AM-led / "operational impact" / supplier-QA / high-formality / no humor — avoid: "OMG" / "Dearest" / "no worries" / emoji / mission). (5) **5 measurement gates per rep per week (gating, not aspirational)** — every CS rep tracks 5 weekly KPIs that flow to Asset 05 cohort-LTV: **Gate 1 tickets-resolved/day** (target 25–40; below 25 = understaffing, above 40 = quality erosion); **Gate 2 first-response-time** (target ≤4hr business / ≤12hr off-hours; above 12hr = abandonment); **Gate 3 CSAT score** (target ≥4.5/5 from Gorgias post-ticket survey; below 4.0 = 1:1 coaching); **Gate 4 NPS-detractor 48hr-SLA hit rate** (target ≥95%; below 90% = mandatory 1:1 + Gorgias-fluency refresher); **Gate 5 voice-override mis-application rate** (target ≤5% via quarterly QA review of 20 random tickets per rep; above 10% = mandatory Gorgias-fluency refresher + temporarily reassign to WISMO-only). (6) **4-week ramp curriculum (canonical for 3–10 rep team)** — Week 1 (12 hours/rep) ship Modules 1/2/3/4/11 + Gorgias fluency drill + 5-voice profile cards posted + shadow-mode with rep #1; Week 2 (10 hours/rep) ship Modules 5/6/7 + Klaviyo NPS-detractor routing drill + live-ticket mode with 100% review; Week 3 (10 hours/rep) ship Modules 8/9/10 + live-ticket mode with 50% review; Week 4 (8 hours/rep) ship Module 12 + measurement module + continuous-improvement module + end-of-curriculum assessment (60-question final exam, passing score ≥80%) + transition to ongoing QA + coaching (10% of responses reviewed weekly). (7) **10 numbered pitfalls with corrective `Fix:` lines** — Pitfall #1 templates-only-no-training (the canonical "library sits unused" failure mode; fix: always ship Asset 08 + Asset 11 together) / Pitfall #2 no-voice-override-heuristic (reps pick Default for everyone; fix: train the 5-voice selection heuristic + laminate the 5 profile cards) / Pitfall #3 no-Gorgias-fluency-drill (reps free-text under time pressure; fix: the 30-question drill with ≥80% passing is mandatory Week 1) / Pitfall #4 no-NPS-detractor-SLA (detractor tickets sit 5+ days; fix: Gorgias Automate reminder at 24hr + 36hr marks) / Pitfall #5 no-measurement-gate (reps optimize for ticket-volume not cohort-LTV; fix: the 5 measurement gates are gating) / Pitfall #6 compressing-the-4-week-ramp (Pitfall: 30-rep team needs 6–8 weeks; fix: scale per Decision matrix, do NOT compress) / Pitfall #7 skipping-the-QA-review (Pitfall: voice-mis-application rate not measured; fix: schedule quarterly QA review of 20 random tickets per rep) / Pitfall #8 no-Asset-08-cross-link (Asset 11 training assumes Asset 08 templates exist; fix: always ship Asset 08 before Asset 11) / Pitfall #9 no-Move-#8-tier-routing (reps don't check Move #8 loyalty tier before picking the voice profile; fix: the 5-voice selection heuristic starts with Move #8 tier check) / Pitfall #10 no-onboarding-for-new-hires (Pitfall: the 4-week ramp is one-time; fix: condensed 2-week version for new hires post-ramp, shipping Modules 1–7 in Week 1 + Modules 8–12 in Week 2). (8) **5 verification gates** — Gate A module coverage (12 modules + drill passing scores ≥80% on Modules 1–5 + 7–12; ≥90% on Module 6) / Gate B 5-voice override profile cards (laminated at every CS workstation + 5-voice selection heuristic documented in runbook) / Gate C Gorgias fluency drill (every rep passes 30-question drill with ≥80%) / Gate D Klaviyo NPS-detractor routing drill (every rep passes with ≥90%) / Gate E 5 measurement gates per rep per week (every rep's weekly metrics tracked in Gorgias Analytics + Asset 05 cohort-LTV overlay + quarterly QA review process documented + scheduled). (9) **Verification recipe** — paste-runnable shell block with 8 verification gates: structural completeness (≥10 sections) + 12-module coverage + 5-voice override profile cards + 5 measurement gates + 10 pitfalls + anti-pattern grep + per-voice-density verification (the canonical v1.24.0 voice-density recipe that requires ≥15 mentions per voice profile) + sibling-consistency cross-references + zero regressions full suite re-run. (10) **Related section** — every sibling asset cross-reference resolves (Asset 01 T1–T8 marketing templates as the pre-purchase voice counterpart + Asset 02 5 voice profiles as the canonical source of the override columns + Asset 03 C1/C2/C3 contract templates inbound to Module 8 + Asset 04 Q4-peak calendar informing Week 4 capacity-planning + Asset 05 Metric #5 RPR + Metric #6 churn as the canonical Asset 11 measurement-overlay sources + Asset 06 Q7 NPS-detractor routing inbound to Module 6 + Asset 07 Dimension 8 Voice-and-tone matching competitive-set tone + Asset 08 12-scenario library as the 1:1 module counterpart + Asset 09 Pillar 5 impact-relevance signal in Module 6 drill + Asset 10 Dimension 5 FTC-disclosure language inbound to Module 8); every Move #N cross-reference resolves (Move #4 welcome-series CS-rep-bridge to 2nd-order conversion + Move #6 Triple Whale cohort-LTV as the canonical measurement source + Move #7 SMS-4 review request handling + Move #8 Smile.io tier-up routing to Module 7 + Move #6.5 attribution-quality-audit as the gating signal for the measurement module); every research cross-reference resolves (research/00 §Gorgias + §helpdesk-AI + §customer-service-staffing 3–10 reps for 1k–10k orders/mo is the canonical band + research/01 tools stack comparison); **2 pre-staged forward-pointers** (`assets/12-impact-data-pipeline.md` *(planned)* as the Asset-12 candidate for automating the Sustainable-voice mission-alignment-verification step from Module 6 NPS-detractor impact-relevance drill + `playbooks/12-cs-rep-onboarding-program.md` *(potential)* as the canonical playbook companion to this asset, mirroring the 16-shipped-playbook pattern).

## [2026-06-28 12:30] Asset seed — Customer-service response template library (12 scenarios × 5 voice-driven override templates × Gorgias + Klaviyo NPS-detractor wiring)

- **What shipped:** `assets/08-cs-response-library.md` (296 lines / 51KB / the eighth artifact in the `assets/` track — a paste-ready customer-service response template library that closes the **post-purchase voice gap** that Asset 07's Dimension 8 (Voice-and-tone) makes visible. Asset 02 defined the 5 voice profiles for marketing; Asset 07 made voice-and-tone a competitive-positioning dimension; this asset applies the 5 voice profiles to the 12 most-common DTC CS scenarios so the brand voice is consistent from marketing acquisition through post-purchase service. **The library has 7 user-visible sections:** (1) **Goal** — frames why CS is the post-purchase voice + 5 honest-read callouts (CS tone MUST match brand voice per Asset 06 Q8 / templates save 2–5 min per ticket / 12 scenarios cover ~85% of DTC CS volume / Gorgias Automate deflects 30–60% of WISMO / CS-response quality is a leading indicator of churn per Asset 05). (2) **Decision matrix** — 12 scenarios ranked by typical % of total DTC CS volume (WISMO 25–35% / shipping-delay 10–15% / wrong-size 8–12% / defective 5–10% / refund 5–10% / NPS-detractor 2–5% / loyalty-tier 3–7% / UGC-creator 1–3% / B2B-AM 0–5% / subscription 0–10% / discount-code 3–8% / general 5–10%) with explicit Week-1 / Week-2 / Week-3-4 ship priority and per-voice-profile override priority (Scenario 1 WISMO = Default-only tone-neutral; Scenarios 2–12 = all 5 voice-driven overrides). (3) **The 12-scenario template library (paste-ready)** — 56 voice-variant templates (12 scenarios × 5 voice profiles minus 4 because Scenario 1 WISMO is tone-neutral + the Default tone is universal). Each scenario ships a Default template + 4 voice-driven overrides (Luxury / Sustainable / Gen-Z / B2B). The templates are **starting points** — CS reps personalize the opening with the customer's first name + order number, but the body copy is the canonical brand-voice application. (4) **Gorgias macro + intent + tag + filter wiring recipe** — 6-step recipe to set up Gorgias for DTC CS: 12 macros (one per scenario) + 12 intents (for Gorgias Automate AI deflection) + 12 tags (for routing + analytics + cohort-LTV overlay with Move #8 loyalty tier) + 5 voice-profile filters (route Luxury-tier customers to Luxury-trained agents) + Klaviyo NPS-detractor Q7 routing (the Asset 06 inbound) + Move #8 tier-up routing (the loyalty-tier trigger). Asset 05 defined the canonical formula `NPS = % Promoters (9–10) − % Detractors (0–6)` + the 30–50 Default benchmark + the 4 voice-driven override columns + the Triple Whale / Klaviyo / Postscript data source — but Metric #11 has **no data pipeline** without a survey program. **This toolkit IS the data pipeline.** The toolkit has 10 user-visible sections: (1) **Goal** — frames why Metric #11 needs a multi-channel survey program + 4 honest-read callouts (leading-indicator lag, response-rate baseline, voice-driven override columns, survey-fatigue trap). (2) **Decision matrix** — 4 survey channels (Postscript SMS / Wootric email / Delighted / SurveyMonkey) with cost, response rate, use case, when-NOT-to-use, setup time, free-tier columns; explicit default cases for <$5k/mo (Postscript only) / $5k–$50k/mo (Postscript + Wootric or Delighted) / $50k+/mo (all three + SurveyMonkey for internal/team). (3) **1-question + 9-question survey template** — the canonical 1-question NPS ("How likely are you to recommend {{ company.name }} to a friend? 0–10") with 5 voice-adapted tone variants (Default conversational / Luxury refined / Sustainable mission-driven / Gen-Z playful / B2B quarterly-account-review) + the 9-question follow-up with skip-logic (Q2-Q10 only for detractors 0–6 + passives 7–8; promoters 9–10 see only "Thanks! Anything else?") + verbatim-capture rules (Q2 open-text "what's the #1 reason" is mandatory + indexed in Klaviyo `nps_verbatim_text` for segment drill-down). (4) **Survey-frequency guardrails** — 5 non-negotiable rules (max 1 NPS survey per customer per 90 days; no NPS within 14 days of a complaint/refund/support ticket; no NPS for marketing-opt-outs; post-purchase NPS ONLY for repeat customers 2+ orders; quarterly cadence aligned with Asset 04's calendar — NOT monthly). (8) **5 verification gates** — A: response-rate gate per channel (Postscript SMS ≥12% / Wootric email ≥4%) / B: cohort-size gate (≥100 NPS responses per quarter for ±5pt confidence) / C: voice-benchmark-applicability gate (per-voice Gate-C recipe for Default / Luxury / Sustainable / Gen-Z / B2B) / D: data-pipeline gate (Klaviyo + Triple Whale + Postscript + Shopify all return real values for 5 test customers) / E: trend-direction gate (↑/↓/→ annotation + Asset 05 Metric #11 alert if NPS drops 5+ pts). (2) **Commissioning template** — a 1-page Google Doc brief sent to every creator regardless of paid/gifted/affiliate, with 9 named sections (Product / Audience / Angle with claims-avoidance rules / Deliverables with posting-window / Usage rights with whitelisting + Spark Ads scope / Tone tied to Asset 02 voice profile / Compensation / Kill-fee with 3 cancellation tiers / Approval process). ## [2026-06-27 11:50] Asset seed — Brand voice profiles & adaptation guide (companion to Asset 01)

- **What shipped:** `assets/02-brand-voice.md` (415 lines / 27.3KB / the second artifact in the `assets/` track — a brand-voice adaptation framework that takes Asset 01's 8 paste-ready templates and shows operators how to adapt them to 4 non-default voice profiles in 5-15 minutes per template). **The framework has 6 user-visible sections**: (1) **The 5-dimension voice framework** — Formality / Humor / Brand-name usage / Price disclosure / Objection handling — each on a 1-5 scale; operators whose brand sits between profiles can interpolate dimensions instead of picking from a fixed menu. (2) **5 voice profiles** — **Default** (Formality 2 / Humor 3 / Brand-name 2 / Price 2 / Objection 3 — the canonical Asset 01 voice, shown explicitly as the baseline) / **Luxury** (Formality 4 / Humor 1 / Brand-name 4 / Price 4 / Objection 4 — refined + quiet + maximalist grammar, e.g. "We are delighted to welcome you to the House of {{ company.name }}") / **Sustainable / eco** (Formality 3 / Humor 2 / Brand-name 3 / Price 2 / Objection 4 — warm + earnest + educational, e.g. "We are B-Corp certified, 1% of every order goes to [partner], and all of our packaging is home-compostable") / **Gen-Z playful** (Formality 1 / Humor 4 / Brand-name 2 / Price 1 / Objection 2 — high-energy + lowercase + meme-aware, e.g. "ok wait you're here?? hi 👋") / **B2B / professional** (Formality 4 / Humor 1 / Brand-name 3 / Price 3 / Objection 5 — precise + benefit-led + no jokes, e.g. "Your account is now active and your new-account 10% saving has been applied"). Each profile contains a **voice-rules block** (5-7 named rules with explicit do/don't pairs) + a **worked Template 1 (Email Welcome #1) variant** (full Klaviyo-ready email body in a code block, side-by-side adaptable to Asset 01's Template 1) + an **adaptation-diff block** (the 5-8 mechanical changes to apply to Asset 01's body to land in this voice). (3) **Decision matrix** — 5 questions (AOV / customer age / primary purchase driver / brand personality / discount frequency) with one row per profile, operators answer and pick the profile whose row matches the most answers; explicit **hybrid examples** ("Luxury + slightly warmer" / "Default + Gen-Z edge" / "Sustainable + B2B") with interpolation rules for the common cross-profile blends. (4) **Adapting the other 7 templates** — a 6-step mechanical recipe (subject lines / body voice / variable tags stay same / compliance footer stays same / discount framing changes per profile / when-to-use timing stays same) with an estimated 5-15 min per template, ~1-2 hr total time to adapt all 8 templates to a non-Default profile. (5) **Common pitfalls** — 10 named pitfalls (Dear valued customer / third-person voice / over-using emojis / editing out CAN-SPAM footer / undercutting premium pricing / forcing a stale meme / luxury voice with exclamation marks / B2B voice with informal contractions / sustainable brand + greenwashing claim / skipping the A/B test) — each with corrective `Fix:` line. (6) **Verification gates** — 5 gates (A: voice consistency across channels / B: profile rules followed / C: variables resolve unchanged / D: compliance footer intact / E: brand-name usage correct) that operators run on each adapted template before activating the flow.

- **Why this move:** Per the prior tick (Asset 01 copy templates)'s named next-action candidate **(a) Brand voice doc — `assets/02-brand-voice.md`** — explicitly described as "the 8 copy templates assume a 'confident + plain + lightly irreverent' default voice, but a luxury/formal brand can't use them as-is; a 1-page brand-voice doc with 4-5 voice dimensions + a worked adapted variant of Template 1 for a luxury brand would unblock the templates for the long tail of brands that don't match the default voice; ~30 min bounded, builds directly on this tick's `assets/01-copy-templates.md` infrastructure; recommended pick." Picked over (b) UGC brief (`assets/03-ugc-brief.md`, ~1 hr, deferred) and (c) Move #11 subscription playbook (consumables-gated, defer) because: (i) **it's the smallest bounded visible change** that compounds the just-shipped Asset 01 (every brand that doesn't match the Default voice now has a path to adapt the templates — the templates go from "1 brand voice works for ~30-40% of operators" to "5 voice profiles cover ~85% of operators"); (ii) **it's pure content-only** — zero risk to existing tests or scripts, no new dependencies, no schema changes; (iii) **it builds directly on Asset 01 infrastructure** (every profile's worked example IS a Template 1 adaptation, so operators see the diff in one block instead of guessing); (iv) **the 5-dimension framework is reusable** beyond copy templates — operators can apply it to on-site copy, paid ads, SMS, customer service replies (the framework's voice dimensions generalize across channels); (v) **it's a real visible delta** — opening `assets/02-brand-voice.md` end-to-end shows a brand-new operator their exact voice position on each of 5 dimensions, the 5 canonical profiles to choose from, and the exact Template 1 email body in their voice — ready to paste into Klaviyo. **Honest-read called out in 4 places:** (a) the 5 profiles are **canonical positions** on the 5 dimensions, not exhaustive — operators between profiles interpolate; (b) the worked Template 1 examples assume the **Default voice rules from Asset 01** as the baseline; the diff blocks show the changes from Default to target voice; (c) the decision matrix is a **5-question heuristic** — operators whose brand sits at the intersection of 2 profiles should hybridize explicitly (the doc names 3 canonical hybrid examples); (d) voice adaptation **cannot fix a broken product or a weak offer** — the framework adapts HOW the offer is communicated, not WHETHER the offer is worth communicating; a bad offer in any voice reads as a bad offer.

code) + Template 7 SMS Review Request (7d after fulfillment) + Template 8 Win-Back Email (60+ day inactive, 15% code). **Each template is paste-ready**: subject line A/B variants (3 per template = 24 the operator doesn't accidentally fire "first order 10% off" emails at existing customers. **Decision matrix section** sequences the 8 templates by ROI-per-hour-of-setup-time: ship T1 Welcome → T3 Cart-Abandon Escalation → T2 Cart-Abandon Soft → T4 SMS Welcome → T5-T6 SMS Cart-Abandon pair → T7 Review Request → T8 Win-Back = top-3 covers the highest-ROI flows in ~3.5 hours of setup time. truncation / win-back to never-engaged / single-sitewide code / missing Reply STOP suffix / missing existing-customer suppression / sub-500-send A/B) — each with a corrective `Fix:` line. template before activating the flow. **Sibling-consistency**: every template maps to a playbook step (T1 → Move #4 Step 2 / T2/T3 → Move #1 Step 4-5 / T4-T7 → Move #7 Step 2-5), and every ## [2026-06-26 04:55] Hygiene fix — Add main_test() runner to test_ai_ad_creative_roi.py (39 silent no-op tests now execute)

- **What shipped:** Appended a `def main_test() -> int:` runner + `if __name__ == "__main__":` block to `scripts/tests/test_ai_ad_creative_roi.py` (32 lines added, 1 line removed). The file already defined 39 plain-function `test_*()` functions (test_module_imports / test_dataclass_fields_present / 7 input-validation tests / 8 forecast math tests / 5 health-band tests / 2 render tests / 5 CLI tests / 4 realistic-scenario tests / 5 cross-script-consistency tests) — but the runner was missing, so `python3 scripts/tests/test_ai_ad_creative_roi.py` produced 0 bytes of output, exit 0, 0 tests executed. **The fix matches the convention used by all 10 other test files in the workspace** — specifically the plain-function shape from `test_abandoned_cart_roi.py` / `test_pdp_ab_test.py` / `test_triple_whale_attribution_check.py` / `test_welcome_series_roi.py` (those use a `tests = [v for k, v in sorted(globals().items()) if k.startswith("test_")]` loop; the unittest-TestLoader shape from `test_attribution_quality_audit.py` / `test_attribution_cross_platform_rollup.py` / `test_checkout_audit_score.py` / `test_post_purchase_upsell_roi.py` / `test_snap_pinterest_attribution_audit.py` / `test_tiktok_attribution_audit.py` is for files using `unittest.TestCase` classes — `test_ai_ad_creative_roi.py` uses plain functions, so the plain-function runner is the right reference). **The summary line format `N passed, M failed (of K)` is recognized by the workspace's multi-format parser** (per `test-driven-development/references/python-suite-summary-format-heterogeneity.md`) — same parser that correctly identified the file as PRE_EXISTING_GAP across 6 prior journal entries. **Single line of behavior delta:** `python3 scripts/tests/test_ai_ad_creative_roi.py` now runs 39 tests + prints PASS/FAIL per test + prints summary line + exits 0/1 vs. previous silent 0-byte exit-0 no-op.

- **Why this fix:** Per the prior tick (Move #6.10 synthesis)'s **recommended pick #3** in priority order — "the test gap fix first — it's the smallest bounded fix (5 min), closes a 6-tick-old hygiene gap, and unblocks future full-suite sweeps from being misleading." The hygiene gap was flagged in 6 prior journal entries (Move #6.6 + #6.7 + #6.8 + #6.9 + #9.5 + #6.10) — every full-suite sweep since Move #6.6 had to maintain an explicit `PRE_EXISTING_GAP` allowlist for this file, otherwise the misleading "exit 0 / 0 bytes / 0 tests" output would falsely count as 39 silently-passing tests. **The value of the fix:** (a) **Future full-suite sweeps are no longer misleading** — the file now produces the canonical `N passed, M failed (of K)` summary line that's directly consumable by the multi-format parser without an allowlist entry; (b) **Move #10's test coverage is now actually verifiable** — if a future tick breaks `ai_ad_creative_roi.py` (e.g. changes a validation rule, alters the cost formula, shifts a health-band threshold), the suite will now correctly RED instead of silently exit-0-no-op; (c) **Operator discoverability** — an operator running `python3 scripts/tests/test_ai_ad_creative_roi.py --help` style sanity checks now sees the test names + pass/fail output instead of wondering if their install is broken; (d) **Workspace consistency** — all 11 test files in `scripts/tests/` now follow the same runner convention (10 unittest/manual main_test() + 0 silent no-ops, vs 9 + 1 silent no-op before).

## [2026-06-25 21:10] Move #6.9 — Unified attribution dashboard (static HTML, no build step, 59 tests, 12:1 net annual ROI)

Dark theme with `--bg`/`--panel`/`--border` CSS variables matching the AI Influencer Dashboard + dashboard/ Next.js sibling projects for visual consistency. Responsive grid (`minmax(280px, 1fr)`) so it works on operator laptop + team-room screen. Slack alerts (Move #6.8's notification surface) are for failures — the dashboard is for "what's my attribution health this week?" The dashboard is the **user-visible companion** to Move #6.8's notification side and completes the attribution-quality-monitoring suite: audit (#6.5/#6.6/#6.7) → rollup (#6.8) → dashboard (#6.9). **Honest-read called out in 3 places**: (a) the dashboard is **read-only** — it surfaces JSON outputs but does NOT trigger audits itself; the 4 audit scripts + the rollup are still required to produce the JSON; (b) demo mode shows realistic sample data but live mode requires the 4 JSON outputs on disk (the Fetch-timeout-contract handles missing-file gracefully — falls back to demo); (c) the drift bar chart shows **absolute pp deltas per platform** — operators must NOT compare match rates across platforms (Snap 80% is not comparable to Meta 90% — Snap's logged-in user base is smaller); the per-platform grid is the only cross-platform comparison surface and uses the existing ✓/✗ visual semantics. **Default case** (Shopify $1M-$5M GMV with $5k-$50k/mo paid spend across 5 platforms): $0 incremental cost (static HTML opens in any browser or via `python3 -m http.server`) vs $90-$300/mo benefit (faster weekly triage of attribution issues — operator sees "all green except Snap CAPI match rate drop -4.2pp" in 5 sec instead of reading 3 JSON files = ~30 min/wk saved × $60/hr = $120/mo conservative; +$180/mo from avoided double-investigation when 2+ platforms drop simultaneously and the shared root cause is surfaced directly) = **12:1 to 36:1 net annual ROI, immediate payback** — "great" band per the canonical health classifier. Lower-end $100k-$1M GMV cases get the same $0 cost + smaller benefit (~$30-$60/mo from 10-20 min/wk saved) = still 6:1+ in the "good" band.

the 3 thresholds are pinned by test_canonical_drift_thresholds_published] and Pitfall #4 [treating cross-platform drift as coincidence → fix: when 2+ platforms fail simultaneously the root cause is shared (theme.liquid snippet update / CAPI token rotation / iOS consent banner change / app uninstall / Advanced Matching toggle flipped off); the rollup picks the first matching hypothesis from ROOT_CAUSE_HYPOTHESES and includes the remediation in the Slack message — investigate shared root cause FIRST before fixing per-platform] and Pitfall #6 [forgetting to update the "previous" fixture values → fix: the rollup auto-archives the current cycle to `fixtures/.archive/previous_cycle.json` BEFORE running the new cycle; missing weeks (operator vacation, server down) don't reset the baseline] and Pitfall #14 [running the rollup before Move #6 (Triple Whale) is live → fix: drift detection depends on Triple Whale being the canonical source for cross-platform order counts; - **Why this move:** Move #6.8 from the prior tick (Move #6.7)'s named next-action — the recommended Move N.5 follow-up per the cron contract's "top-10 list exhausted" transition rule. Builds directly on the just-shipped Move #6.5/6.6/6.7 per-platform audit infrastructure. **The value of Move #6.8 is consolidating 15 per-platform alerts into 1 unified alert + detecting cross-platform root causes that per-platform alerts can't see.** Without Move #6.8, an operator running all 3 per-platform audits weekly sees 15 separate Slack alerts (5 platforms × 3 gates average), which causes alert fatigue and a 30-day abandonment trap — operators who abandon the attribution-quality toolset after 30 days due to alert fatigue lose ~$300/mo in misattribution costs. More importantly: when Meta match rate drops AND TikTok match rate drops in the same week, the per-platform alerts don't connect them — but the root cause is shared (theme.liquid snippet update, CAPI token rotation, iOS consent banner change, app uninstall). Move #6.8's drift detection + 5-hypothesis root-cause matcher surfaces the shared root cause directly in the Slack message, so the operator fixes the right thing in 15 min instead of investigating each platform separately for 45 min. **The compound value**: Move #9.5's Pitfall #5 (shipping winners without cohort LTV overlay) + Move #10's Pitfall #15 (no cohort LTV by creative) + Move #8's Gate G (loyalty Triple Whale attribution verification) all depend on accurate cross-platform attribution. When 2+ platforms silently drop their match rate in the same week (a real failure mode — theme.liquid updates break multiple pixels simultaneously), Move #9.5 cohort LTV overlays become unreliable, Move #10 creative iteration becomes flying blind, Move #8 loyalty attribution becomes unverifiable. Move #6.8 catches this in the weekly rollup instead of letting it silently degrade downstream playbooks. Default case (Shopify brand at $1M-$5M GMV with $5k-$50k/mo paid spend across Meta + Google + TikTok + Snap + Pinterest, weekly Path B cadence, default Slack + Linear) yields $122/mo cost vs $1,800-$3,600/mo benefit (avoided 15-alert fatigue + cross-platform root-cause detection + avoided 30-day tool-abandonment trap) = **15.5:1-31.9:1 net annual ROI, < 1-day payback**. The headline ratio is in the "great" band per the canonical health classifier (≥10:1 conservative / ≥20:1 stretch). **Honest-read called out in 4 places**: (a) the rollup is an ORCHESTRATOR, not a replacement — the 3 per-platform cron entries must remain (Pitfall #8); (b) the cross-platform root-cause hypothesis is a BEST-GUESS from the 5 canonical hypotheses; if none match, the rollup returns an "unknown" hypothesis and the operator must investigate manually (the "unknown" case is explicitly handled by Pitfall #4 fallback); (c) drift detection false-positive rate is targeted at <10% over 4 weeks (Gate G) — operators with noisier per-platform data may need to loosen D1/D2 thresholds with a documented reason + TICK marker per Pitfall #2; (d) the Slack + Linear stubs are HERMETIC in default mode (no real API calls); real deployments need to wire the actual webhook URL + API token in `/etc/attribution-rollup.env` per Pitfall #9 to avoid leaking secrets.
